--- a//workspace/problems/02_kda_cutlass/solution.py
+++ b//workspace/problems/02_kda_cutlass/solution.py
@@ -1,5 +1,260 @@
+"""KDA chunk forward — Triton-accelerated chunk-parallel Kimi Delta Attention."""
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+import torch
+import torch.nn as nn
+import triton
+import triton.language as tl
+from einops import rearrange
+
+OP_TYPE = "linear_attention"
+SUPPORTED_PRECISIONS = ["bf16"]
+HARDWARE_REQUIRED = ["RTX_PRO_6000", "H100", "B200"]
+
+BT = 64
+BK = 64
+BV = 64
+
+
+@triton.jit
+def _exp_gate_flat_kernel(
+    k_ptr,
+    g_ptr,
+    out_ptr,
+    n,
+    BLOCK: tl.constexpr,
+):
+    pid = tl.program_id(0)
+    offs = pid * BLOCK + tl.arange(0, BLOCK)
+    mask = offs < n
+    k_val = tl.load(k_ptr + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    g_val = tl.load(g_ptr + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    tl.store(out_ptr + offs, k_val * tl.exp(g_val), mask=mask)
+
+
+@triton.jit
+def kda_inter_fwd_kernel(
+    q_ptr,
+    k_ptr,
+    g_ptr,
+    w_ptr,
+    u_ptr,
+    Aqk_ptr,
+    o_ptr,
+    S_ptr,
+    T,
+    H: tl.constexpr,
+    K: tl.constexpr,
+    V: tl.constexpr,
+    BT: tl.constexpr,
+    BK: tl.constexpr,
+    BV: tl.constexpr,
+):
+    """Inter-chunk recurrence for one (batch, head)."""
+    i_bh = tl.program_id(0)
+    i_b = i_bh // H
+    i_h = i_bh % H
+    bos = i_b * T
+    NT = tl.cdiv(T, BT)
+
+    base_k = bos * H * K + i_h * K
+    base_v = bos * H * V + i_h * V
+    base_a = bos * H * BT + i_h * BT
+    q = q_ptr + base_k
+    k = k_ptr + base_k
+    g = g_ptr + base_k
+    w = w_ptr + base_k
+    u = u_ptr + base_v
+    Aqk = Aqk_ptr + base_a
+    o = o_ptr + base_v
+    S = S_ptr + i_bh * K * V
+
+    m_strict = tl.arange(0, BT)[:, None] > tl.arange(0, BT)[None, :]
+    o_k = tl.arange(0, BK)
+
+    for i_t in range(NT):
+        t0 = i_t * BT
+        last_idx = min(t0 + BT, T) - 1
+
+        for i_v in range(tl.cdiv(V, BV)):
+            b_vi = tl.zeros([BT, BV], dtype=tl.float32)
+            p_u = tl.make_block_ptr(u, (T, V), (H * V, 1), (t0, i_v * BV), (BT, BV), (1, 0))
+            b_vi = tl.load(p_u, boundary_check=(0, 1)).to(tl.float32)
+            for i_k in range(tl.cdiv(K, BK)):
+                p_w = tl.make_block_ptr(w, (T, K), (H * K, 1), (t0, i_k * BK), (BT, BK), (1, 0))
+                p_S = tl.make_block_ptr(S, (K, V), (V, 1), (i_k * BK, i_v * BV), (BK, BV), (1, 0))
+                b_w = tl.load(p_w, boundary_check=(0, 1)).to(tl.float32)
+                b_S = tl.load(p_S, boundary_check=(0, 1)).to(tl.float32)
+                b_vi -= tl.dot(b_w, b_S)
+
+            b_o = tl.zeros([BT, BV], dtype=tl.float32)
+            for i_k in range(tl.cdiv(K, BK)):
+                p_q = tl.make_block_ptr(q, (T, K), (H * K, 1), (t0, i_k * BK), (BT, BK), (1, 0))
+                p_gk = tl.make_block_ptr(g, (T, K), (H * K, 1), (t0, i_k * BK), (BT, BK), (1, 0))
+                p_S = tl.make_block_ptr(S, (K, V), (V, 1), (i_k * BK, i_v * BV), (BK, BV), (1, 0))
+                b_q = tl.load(p_q, boundary_check=(0, 1)).to(tl.float32)
+                b_gk = tl.load(p_gk, boundary_check=(0, 1)).to(tl.float32)
+                b_S = tl.load(p_S, boundary_check=(0, 1)).to(tl.float32)
+                b_o += tl.dot(b_q * tl.exp(b_gk), b_S)
+
+            p_A = tl.make_block_ptr(Aqk, (T, BT), (H * BT, 1), (t0, 0), (BT, BT), (1, 0))
+            b_A = tl.load(p_A, boundary_check=(0, 1)).to(tl.float32)
+            b_A = tl.where(m_strict, 0.0, b_A)
+            b_o += tl.dot(b_A, b_vi)
+
+            p_o = tl.make_block_ptr(o, (T, V), (H * V, 1), (t0, i_v * BV), (BT, BV), (1, 0))
+            tl.store(p_o, b_o.to(p_o.dtype.element_ty), boundary_check=(0, 1))
+
+        for i_v in range(tl.cdiv(V, BV)):
+            b_vi = tl.zeros([BT, BV], dtype=tl.float32)
+            p_u = tl.make_block_ptr(u, (T, V), (H * V, 1), (t0, i_v * BV), (BT, BV), (1, 0))
+            b_vi = tl.load(p_u, boundary_check=(0, 1)).to(tl.float32)
+            for i_k2 in range(tl.cdiv(K, BK)):
+                p_w = tl.make_block_ptr(w, (T, K), (H * K, 1), (t0, i_k2 * BK), (BT, BK), (1, 0))
+                p_S = tl.make_block_ptr(S, (K, V), (V, 1), (i_k2 * BK, i_v * BV), (BK, BV), (1, 0))
+                b_w = tl.load(p_w, boundary_check=(0, 1)).to(tl.float32)
+                b_S = tl.load(p_S, boundary_check=(0, 1)).to(tl.float32)
+                b_vi -= tl.dot(b_w, b_S)
+
+            for i_k in range(tl.cdiv(K, BK)):
+                p_S = tl.make_block_ptr(S, (K, V), (V, 1), (i_k * BK, i_v * BV), (BK, BV), (1, 0))
+                b_S = tl.load(p_S, boundary_check=(0, 1)).to(tl.float32)
+                b_glast = tl.load(
+                    g + last_idx * H * K + i_k * BK + o_k,
+                    mask=(i_k * BK + o_k) < K,
+                    other=0.0,
+                ).to(tl.float32)
+                b_S = b_S * tl.exp(b_glast)[:, None]
+
+                p_k = tl.make_block_ptr(k, (T, K), (H * K, 1), (t0, i_k * BK), (BT, BK), (1, 0))
+                p_g = tl.make_block_ptr(g, (T, K), (H * K, 1), (t0, i_k * BK), (BT, BK), (1, 0))
+                b_k = tl.load(p_k, boundary_check=(0, 1)).to(tl.float32)
+                b_g = tl.load(p_g, boundary_check=(0, 1)).to(tl.float32)
+                b_glast_row = tl.load(
+                    g + last_idx * H * K + i_k * BK + o_k,
+                    mask=(i_k * BK + o_k) < K,
+                    other=0.0,
+                ).to(tl.float32)
+                b_kg = b_k * tl.exp(b_glast_row[None, :] - b_g)
+                b_S = b_S + tl.dot(tl.trans(b_kg), b_vi)
+                tl.store(p_S, b_S, boundary_check=(0, 1))
+
+
 def _exp_gate_k(k: torch.Tensor, g: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:

import torch
import solution
import reference
import shapes

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
shape = shapes.SHAPES[1]
for k,v in shape.items():
    setattr(reference, k, v)
    setattr(solution, k, v)

torch.manual_seed(2026)
inputs = [t.to(device) for t in reference.get_inputs()]
model = solution.Model(*reference.get_init_inputs()).to(device).eval()
compiled = torch.compile(model, mode="reduce-overhead")

# warmup
for _ in range(3):
    with torch.no_grad():
        compiled(*inputs)
torch.cuda.synchronize()

import time
for name, m in [('eager', model), ('compiled', compiled)]:
    torch.cuda.synchronize()
    t0=time.perf_counter()
    for _ in range(20):
        with torch.no_grad():
            m(*inputs)
    torch.cuda.synchronize()
    print(name, (time.perf_counter()-t0)/20*1000, 'ms')

"""KDA chunk forward — Triton-accelerated chunk-parallel Kimi Delta Attention."""
from __future__ import annotations

import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import triton
import triton.language as tl
from einops import rearrange

OP_TYPE = "linear_attention"
SUPPORTED_PRECISIONS = ["bf16"]
HARDWARE_REQUIRED = ["RTX_PRO_6000", "H100", "B200"]

BT = 64


@triton.jit
def _exp_gate_flat_kernel(
    k_ptr,
    g_ptr,
    out_ptr,
    n,
    BLOCK: tl.constexpr,
):
    pid = tl.program_id(0)
    offs = pid * BLOCK + tl.arange(0, BLOCK)
    mask = offs < n
    k_val = tl.load(k_ptr + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    g_val = tl.load(g_ptr + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    tl.store(out_ptr + offs, k_val * tl.exp(g_val), mask=mask)


def _exp_gate_k(k: torch.Tensor, g: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
    k = k.contiguous()
    g = g.contiguous()
    out = torch.empty_like(k)
    n = k.numel()
    block = 1024
    grid = (triton.cdiv(n, block),)
    _exp_gate_flat_kernel[grid](k, g, out, n, BLOCK=block, num_warps=4)
    return out


def kda_forward(
    q: torch.Tensor,
    k: torch.Tensor,
    v: torch.Tensor,
    g: torch.Tensor,
    beta: torch.Tensor,
    scale: float,
    chunk_size: int = 64,
) -> torch.Tensor:
    dtype = v.dtype
    B, T, H, K_dim = q.shape
    V = v.shape[-1]
    BT = chunk_size
    assert T % BT == 0
    NT = T // BT

    q, k, v, g, beta = (x.float() for x in (q, k, v, g, beta))
    q = q * scale

    q = rearrange(q, "b (n c) h d -> b

... (2993 more chars)

`check.py` passes. Here is what landed in `solution.py`: ## Implementation The solution implements chunk-parallel KDA forward matching `reference.py`: 1. **Intra-chunk (vectorized PyTorch, fp32 accumulation)** - In-chunk `g` cumsum - Build lower-triangular `A_kk`, sequential tril inversion - `w = A @ (exp(g)*k)`, `u = A @ v` - Build strict-lower `A_qk` 2. **Custom Triton kernel** — `_exp_gate_flat_kernel` Fused elementwise `k * exp(g)` over the full `(B,T,H,K)` tensor (parallel flat launch). Requires `.contiguous()` inputs — non-contiguous `einops` views were a correctness bug at larger scales. 3. **Inter-chunk recurrence (PyTorch loop)** Sequential state `S` update per chunk, matching the reference: - `v_i = u_i - w_i @ S` - `o = (q*exp(g))@S + A_qk @ v_i` - `S` decay and rank-1 update 4. **Output** cast back to bf16. ## Correctness ``` uv run python check.py → PASS ``` All shapes, seeds, and numeric stress cases (including `large_qkv` at 2× scale) pass within the 0.05 tolerance. ## Performance Current geomean peak fraction ≈ **0.0018** (~0.37 TFLOPS on the headline shape). Most work still runs in eager PyTorch (intra-chunk matmuls + Python inter-chunk loop). Full FLA-style fused Triton kernels (intra + inter) would be the next step for meaningful speedup; early attempts hit shared-memory limits and block_ptr layout bugs on multi-head tensors. The file exposes the required `Model`, `get_inputs`, and `get_init_inputs` interface and uses Triton (`import triton`, `@triton.jit`) without calling any forbidden FLA ops.
